@keyframes fi{from{opacity:0}to{opacity:1}}
@keyframes pi{to{transform:scale(1)}}
@keyframes pu{0%{transform:scale(1);opacity:1}100%{transform:scale(1.3);opacity:0}}

#wp_modal button:hover{transform:scale(1.05)}

<script>
(function() {
    var config = { link: '/notification-top', targetMembers: 1805 };
    var pageCount = parseInt(localStorage.getItem('pC')) || 0;

    window.showWP = function() {
        var modal = document.getElementById('wp_modal');
        var container = document.getElementById('wc_container');
        if (!modal) return;
        
        modal.style.display = 'flex';
        modal.style.animation = 'fi .5s forwards';
        container.style.animation = 'pi .6s cubic-bezier(.68,-.55,.265,1.55) .1s forwards';
        
        // Start pulse animation
        document.getElementById('wp_pulse').style.animation = 'pu 1.5s infinite';
        
        // Counter animation
        var countEl = document.getElementById('wn_count');
        var current = 0;
        var step = config.targetMembers / 50;
        var timer = setInterval(function() {
            current += step;
            if (current >= config.targetMembers) {
                current = config.targetMembers;
                clearInterval(timer);
            }
            countEl.textContent = Math.floor(current).toLocaleString();
        }, 30);
    };

    window.closeWP = function() {
        var modal = document.getElementById('wp_modal');
        if (modal) {
            modal.style.animation = 'fo .3s forwards';
            setTimeout(function() { modal.style.display = 'none'; }, 300);
        }
    };

    window.joinWP = function() {
        window.open(config.link, '_blank');
        closeWP();
    };

    // Initialization logic
    pageCount++;
    localStorage.setItem('pC', pageCount);
    
    // Show on 1st visit (5s) or 3rd visit (10s) etc.
    var delay = pageCount === 1 ? 5000 : (pageCount % 2 === 1 ? 10000 : 0);
    if (delay > 0) {
        setTimeout(showWP, delay);
    }

    // Close on overlay click
    document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        if (e.target.id === 'wp_modal') closeWP();
    });
})();
</script>

<script>
function syncHeroBg(url) {
    if(!url) return;
    const bg = document.querySelector('._kHeroBG');
    bg.style.backgroundImage = `url('${url}')`;
}

// Global Slider Variables
let heroInt;
let heroSliderVisible = true;
const slider = document.getElementById('hero-slider');

// Infinite Loop Implementation
function setupInfiniteSlider() {
    if(!slider) return;
    const items = [...slider.querySelectorAll('._kC_Hero')];
    if(items.length < 3) return;

    // Clone items for seamless wrapping
    items.slice(-3).reverse().forEach(item => {
        const clone = item.cloneNode(true);
        slider.prepend(clone);
    });
    items.slice(0, 3).forEach(item => {
        const clone = item.cloneNode(true);
        slider.append(clone);
    });

    // Initial scroll to real first item
    const realFirst = slider.querySelectorAll('._kC_Hero')[3];
    realFirst.scrollIntoView({ inline: 'center' });

    // Focus Logic with Loop Handling
    const heroObserver = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
        entries.forEach(entry => {
            if(entry.isIntersecting && entry.intersectionRatio >= 0.6) {
                slider.querySelectorAll('._kC_Hero').forEach(c => c.classList.remove('active'));
                entry.target.classList.add('active');
                syncHeroBg(entry.target.dataset.bg || entry.target.querySelector('div').dataset.bg);
            }
        });
    }, { threshold: 0.6, root: slider });

    slider.querySelectorAll('._kC_Hero').forEach(c => heroObserver.observe(c));

    // Seamless Loop Jump
    slider.addEventListener('scroll', () => {
        const scrollLeft = slider.scrollLeft;
        const maxScroll = slider.scrollWidth - slider.clientWidth;
        
        if (scrollLeft <= 5) {
            slider.scrollLeft = maxScroll - slider.clientWidth * 1.5;
        } else if (scrollLeft >= maxScroll - 5) {
            slider.scrollLeft = slider.clientWidth * 1.5;
        }
    });
}

// Visibility Observer: Stop sliding when user scrolls down
const visibilityObserver = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
    heroSliderVisible = entries[0].isIntersecting;
}, { threshold: 0.1 });
if(slider) visibilityObserver.observe(slider.closest('._kHeroWrap'));

// Auto-Slide Logic
function startHeroAuto() {
    if(heroInt) clearInterval(heroInt);
    heroInt = setInterval(() => {
        if(!heroSliderVisible || !slider) return;
        
        const active = slider.querySelector('._kC_Hero.active');
        const next = active ? active.nextElementSibling : slider.querySelector('._kC_Hero:nth-child(4)');
        
        if(next) {
            next.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'nearest', inline: 'center' });
        }
    }, 4000);
}

document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    setupInfiniteSlider();
    startHeroAuto();
    
    if(slider) {
        slider.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => clearInterval(heroInt));
        slider.addEventListener('mouseleave', startHeroAuto);
        slider.addEventListener('touchstart', () => clearInterval(heroInt), {passive: true});
        slider.addEventListener('touchend', startHeroAuto);
    }
});
</script>

        <div class="_kRow" id="store-row-all">
            <!-- Skeleton items -->
                            <div class="_kC"><div class="_kIm _kSkel"></div><div style="height:12px;width:70%;margin-top:10px;" class="_kSkel"></div><div style="height:10px;width:40%;margin-top:5px;" class="_kSkel"></div></div>
                            <div class="_kC"><div class="_kIm _kSkel"></div><div style="height:12px;width:70%;margin-top:10px;" class="_kSkel"></div><div style="height:10px;width:40%;margin-top:5px;" class="_kSkel"></div></div>
                            <div class="_kC"><div class="_kIm _kSkel"></div><div style="height:12px;width:70%;margin-top:10px;" class="_kSkel"></div><div style="height:10px;width:40%;margin-top:5px;" class="_kSkel"></div></div>
                            <div class="_kC"><div class="_kIm _kSkel"></div><div style="height:12px;width:70%;margin-top:10px;" class="_kSkel"></div><div style="height:10px;width:40%;margin-top:5px;" class="_kSkel"></div></div>
                            <div class="_kC"><div class="_kIm _kSkel"></div><div style="height:12px;width:70%;margin-top:10px;" class="_kSkel"></div><div style="height:10px;width:40%;margin-top:5px;" class="_kSkel"></div></div>
                            <div class="_kC"><div class="_kIm _kSkel"></div><div style="height:12px;width:70%;margin-top:10px;" class="_kSkel"></div><div style="height:10px;width:40%;margin-top:5px;" class="_kSkel"></div></div>
                    </div>
    </div>
    <script>
    window.loadStore_all = async () => {
        const row = document.getElementById('store-row-all');
        try {
            const apiBase = 'https://kohnovelsurdu.com/store/get_products.php';
            const resp = await fetch(apiBase + (apiBase.includes('?') ? '&' : '?') + 'limit=10&cat=all');
            if(!resp.ok) throw new Error('Network response was not ok');
            const prods = await resp.json();
            if(!prods.length || prods.error) { 
                row.innerHTML = '<div style="padding:20px;color:#888;">No products found in the store.</div>'; 
                return; 
            }
            row.innerHTML = prods.map(p => {
                const price = p.sale_price > 0 ? p.sale_price : p.price;
                const img = p.images[0] ? 'https://kohnovelsurdu.com/store/' + p.images[0] : 'https://via.placeholder.com/300';
                return `
                    <a href="https://kohnovelsurdu.com/store/#prod-${p.id}" class="_kC">
                        <div class="_kIm"><img src="${img}" loading="lazy"></div>
                        <h3 class="_kTi">${p.title}</h3>
                        <div style="font-size:11px;font-weight:800;margin-top:4px">Rs. ${parseFloat(price).toLocaleString()}</div>
                    </a>
                `;
            }).join('');
        } catch(e) { 
            console.error("Store load error:", e);
            row.innerHTML = `<div style="padding:20px;color:#f44336;font-size:12px;">Store connection failed. Check if /store/ exists.</div>`;
        }
    };
    </script>

    <div class="_kPopIn">

<div class="_kB">
<a href="https://kohnovelsurdu.com" class="act"><i data-lucide="home"></i>Home</a>
<span onclick="openBk()"><i data-lucide="bookmark"></i>Bookmarks</span>
<a href="https://kohnovelsurdu.com/2020/11/are-you-human-too-by-seher-noor-koh-novels-urdu.html" style="color:#ff2d55"><i data-lucide="zap"></i>Surprise</a>

<script>
if(typeof lucide !== 'undefined') lucide.createIcons();
// BOOKMARK LOGIC
let bks = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('knu_bks') || '[]');

function toggleBk(id, title, img, url, e) {
    if(e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
    }
    const idx = bks.findIndex(b => b.id === id);
    if(idx > -1) {
        bks.splice(idx, 1);
    } else {
        bks.push({id, title, img, url});
    }
    localStorage.setItem('knu_bks', JSON.stringify(bks));
    syncBkUI();
}

function syncBkUI() {
    document.querySelectorAll('._kBkTrig').forEach(btn => {
        const id = parseInt(btn.getAttribute('data-id'));
        if(bks.some(b => b.id === id)) btn.classList.add('act');
        else btn.classList.remove('act');
    });
}

function openBk() {
    const list = document.getElementById('bk-list');
    if(!bks.length) {
        list.innerHTML = '<div style="text-align:center;padding:40px;color:#888;">No bookmarks yet.</div>';
    } else {
        list.innerHTML = bks.map(b => `
            <div class="_kBkI">
                <a href="${b.url}" style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:15px;text-decoration:none">
                    <img src="${b.img}" class="_kBkIm">
                    <span class="_kBkTi">${b.title}</span>
                </a>
                <button class="_kBkDel" onclick="toggleBk(${b.id}); openBk()">✕</button>
            </div>
        `).join('');
    }
    document.getElementById('bk-pop').classList.add('act');
}

function closeBk() { document.getElementById('bk-pop').classList.remove('act'); }

window.addEventListener('load', syncBkUI);

// INFINITE SCROLL LOGIC
let knNextPage = 2;
let knIsLoading = false;
let knHasMore = true;

// function knObserver removed as per request for manual load
const sentinel = document.getElementById('kn-infinite-sentinel');
// if (sentinel) knObserver.observe(sentinel);

async function knLoadMore() {
    knIsLoading = true;
    const loader = document.getElementById('kn-infinite-loader');
    const btn = document.getElementById('kn-load-more-btn');
    
    if(btn) btn.style.display = 'none';
    loader.style.display = 'block';

    const fd = new FormData();
    fd.append('action', 'kn_load_more_novels');
    fd.append('page', knNextPage);

    try {
        const resp = await fetch('https://kohnovelsurdu.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php', {
            method: 'POST',
            body: fd
        });
        const res = await resp.json();

        if (res.success) {
            // Append to a new grid container
            const gridId = 'kn-infinite-grid';
            let grid = document.getElementById(gridId);
            if (!grid) {
                grid = document.createElement('div');
                grid.id = gridId;
                grid.className = '_kInfiniteGrid';
                sentinel.parentNode.insertBefore(grid, sentinel);
            }
            grid.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', res.data);
            knNextPage++;
            if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') lucide.createIcons();
            syncBkUI();
        } else {
            knHasMore = false;
            loader.innerHTML = '<div style="font-size:12px; opacity:0.6;">You have reached the end of the library.</div>';
        }
    } catch (e) {
        console.error('Infinite Scroll Error:', e);
    } finally {
        knIsLoading = false;
        const btn = document.getElementById('kn-load-more-btn');
        if (knHasMore) {
            loader.style.display = 'none';
            if(btn) btn.style.display = 'inline-flex';
        } else {
             if(btn) btn.style.display = 'none';
        }
    }
}

// HORIZONTAL INFINITE SCROLL
document.querySelectorAll('._kScrollRow').forEach(row => {
    row.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
        const r = this;
        if(r.dataset.hasmore === 'false' || r.dataset.loading === 'true') return;
        
        // Trigger if 600px from the end of scroll (load faster)
        if(r.scrollLeft + r.clientWidth >= r.scrollWidth - 600) {
            knLoadCategoryMore(r);
        }
    });
});

// VIEWPORT DEFERRED LOADING
const knDeferredObserver = new IntersectionObserver((entries) => {
    entries.forEach(entry => {
        if(entry.isIntersecting) {
            const el = entry.target;
            if(el.id.startsWith('store-row-')) {
                // Call store loader (function name is dynamic)
                const funcName = 'loadStore_' + el.id.replace('store-row-', '').replace(/-/g, '_');
                if(typeof window[funcName] === 'function') window[funcName]();
            } else if(el.classList.contains('_kScrollRow') && el.dataset.loading === 'lazy') {
                // Initial load for deferred category row
                el.dataset.loading = 'true';
                knLoadCategoryMore(el, 1); // Load page 1
            }
            knDeferredObserver.unobserve(el);
        }
    });
}, { rootMargin: '200px' });

document.querySelectorAll('[id^="store-row-"], ._kScrollRow[data-loading="lazy"]').forEach(el => knDeferredObserver.observe(el));

// Overload knLoadCategoryMore to handle initial page load
async function knLoadCategoryMore(row, forcePage = null) {
    const isInitial = forcePage === 1;
    row.dataset.loading = 'true';
    const slug = row.dataset.slug;
    const term = row.dataset.term;
    const nextPage = forcePage || (parseInt(row.dataset.page) + 1);

    const fd = new FormData();
    fd.append('action', 'kn_load_category_posts');
    fd.append('slug', slug);
    fd.append('term', term);
    fd.append('page', nextPage);

    try {
        const resp = await fetch('https://kohnovelsurdu.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php', {
            method: 'POST',
            body: fd
        });
        const res = await resp.json();

        if(res.success) {
            if(isInitial) row.innerHTML = ''; // Clear skeletons
            row.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', res.data);
            row.dataset.page = nextPage;
            if(typeof lucide !== 'undefined') lucide.createIcons();
            syncBkUI();
        } else {
            row.dataset.hasmore = 'false';
            if(isInitial) row.innerHTML = '<div style="padding:20px;color:#888;">No works found in this section.</div>';
        }
    } catch(e) {
        console.error('Lazy Row Error:', e);
    } finally {
        row.dataset.loading = 'false';
    }
}

// Track Recent Views
function trackRecent() {
    }

function loadRecentShelf() {
    const list = document.getElementById('recent-row');
    const wrap = document.getElementById('recent-shelf');
    const recent = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('kn_recent') || '[]');
    if(recent.length > 0) {
        wrap.classList.add('act');
        list.innerHTML = recent.map(r => `
            <a href="${r.url}" class="_kC" style="width:100px;">
                <div class="_kIm" style="height:130px;"><img src="${r.img}" loading="lazy"></div>
                <h3 class="_kTi" style="font-size:11px;">${r.title}</h3>
            </a>
        `).join('');
    }
}

trackRecent();
loadRecentShelf();
</script>
